### DAY 5 — Workplace Conflicts & Negotiation
**Grammar Focus:** Advanced Reported Speech (insist, recommend, deny, suggest)

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Workplace conflicts, negosiasi, dan cara melaporkan apa yang dikatakan orang lain dalam konteks profesional yang sensitif — komplain ke HR, negosiasi gaji, atau mediasi konflik tim.

**Grammar Pendukung — Advanced Reported Speech**

Day 5 mengembangkan Reported Speech ke level lebih advanced: reporting verbs seperti insist, recommend, deny, suggest, yang masing-masing punya struktur grammar berbeda (banyak yang pakai subjunctive/bare infinitive, bukan backshift tense biasa).

Pola:
- **insist/recommend/suggest + that + subject + bare infinitive (subjunctive):** She insisted that he apologize immediately.
- **deny + gerund:** He denied missing the deadline.
- **suggest + gerund (alternatif):** She suggested rescheduling the meeting.

Contoh lengkap:
- The manager recommended that the team meet earlier next time.
- He denied saying anything offensive during the meeting.
- She insisted that the contract be reviewed before signing.

**Kontras dengan Day 4 (Passive + Modals):** Day 4 fokus ke menghilangkan pelaku aksi demi objektivitas akademik. Day 5 fokus ke melaporkan ucapan/pendapat orang lain secara akurat dalam konteks konflik — disini siapa yang mengatakan apa justru jadi pusat perhatian, bukan dihilangkan. Error umum: user menambahkan "to" setelah subjunctive bare infinitive (salah: "insisted that he to apologize", benar: "insisted that he apologize"), atau memakai gerund setelah "insist" padahal pola standarnya bare infinitive.

**Catatan:** Subjunctive ini gak ada bentuk yang persis sama di Bahasa Indonesia — orang Indonesia cenderung menambahkan "should" karena di Indonesia menerjemahkan insisted as "bersikukuh agar harus" → ini menjelaskan kenapa error "insisted that he should apologize" (sebenarnya boleh tapi lebih formal British English, bukan error fatal) sering muncul.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Reporting verbs ini krusial untuk dokumentasi formal di tempat kerja — laporan insiden, email follow-up setelah rapat, atau ringkasan negosiasi yang butuh akurasi siapa-bilang-apa.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| dispute /dɪˈspjuːt/ | a disagreement or argument | — |
| compromise /ˈkɒmprəmaɪz/ | an agreement reached by both sides giving up something | — |
| grievance /ˈɡriːvəns/ | a formal complaint about unfair treatment | — |
| escalate /ˈɛskəleɪt/ | to make a conflict more serious or intense | — |
| mediate /ˈmiːdieɪt/ | to help resolve a conflict between two parties | — |
| confront /kənˈfrʌnt/ | to face someone directly about a problem | — |
| accountability /əˌkaʊntəˈbɪləti/ | responsibility for one's actions or decisions | — |
| ultimatum /ˌʌltɪˈmeɪtəm/ | a final demand with a threatened consequence | — |
| leverage /ˈlɛvərɪdʒ/ | (noun) power or influence used to gain an advantage | — |
| concede /kənˈsiːd/ | to admit something is true, often reluctantly | — |
| stand one's ground /stænd wʌnz ɡraʊnd/ | to refuse to change one's position under pressure | — |
| back down /bæk daʊn/ | to withdraw from a position or demand | — |
| come to terms (with) /kʌm tuː tɜːrmz/ | to reach an agreement, or to accept a difficult situation | — |
| iron out /ˈaɪərn aʊt/ | to resolve small problems through discussion | Bukan "menyetrika" — idiom artinya "menyelesaikan masalah kecil" |
| breakthrough /ˈbreɪkθruː/ | a sudden important development or solution | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: menambahkan "to" setelah subjunctive bare infinitive).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 4 (hypothesis, methodology, peer review, replicate, empirical, variable, significant, findings, publication, bias, draw a conclusion, rule out, carry out research, validate, inconclusive) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal nuance pemilihan reporting verb (insist vs recommend vs suggest) sesuai konteks formalitas.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks negosiasi/konflik kerja.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "reach a compromise", "stand one's ground", "iron out the details". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval advanced reported speech (contoh: "What did your manager recommend last time there was a conflict in your team?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi keberanian user menulis tentang topik konflik yang kadang terasa sensitif — tone humble, validasi bahwa subjunctive memang salah satu struktur paling tidak intuitif buat penutur Bahasa Indonesia, jadi progress kecil pun layak diapresiasi.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat reported speech secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke pelafalan subjunctive bare infinitive yang sering salah ditambahkan "to" atau "-s" oleh pemula.

### DAY 6 — Travel Mishaps & Cultural Misunderstandings Abroad
**Grammar Focus:** Participle Clauses (reduced relative/adverbial)
🌉 *Overlap topic: Travel sudah muncul di A1/A2/B1 — di B2, fokusnya bergeser dari survival phrases ke storytelling yang lebih kompleks lewat reduced clauses.*

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Travel mishaps (kehilangan paspor, salah naik kereta, miskomunikasi budaya) dan cultural misunderstandings yang terjadi saat traveling ke negara asing.

**Grammar Pendukung — Participle Clauses**

Day 6 memperkenalkan Participle Clauses — cara meringkas relative clause atau adverbial clause menggunakan -ing (present participle) atau -ed/V3 (past participle), umum dipakai untuk membuat narasi lebih ringkas dan natural.

Pola:
- **Reduced relative clause:** The tourist standing at the gate (= who was standing) looked confused.
- **Reduced adverbial clause (reason/time):** Having lost his passport, he had to visit the embassy. (= Because he had lost...)
- **Passive participle:** Confused by the local customs, she accidentally offended her host. (= Because she was confused...)

**Kontras dengan Day 5 (Advanced Reported Speech):** Day 5 fokus ke akurasi melaporkan ucapan orang lain dengan reporting verb khusus. Day 6 fokus ke meringkas dua kalimat/clause jadi satu kalimat yang lebih ringkas dan mengalir — bukan soal siapa-bilang-apa, tapi soal efisiensi struktur kalimat naratif. Error umum: user lupa mengubah subject di kedua clause harus sama sebelum di-reduce (tidak bisa direduce kalau subjectnya beda), atau salah pilih -ing vs -ed (aktif vs pasif).

**Catatan:** Bahasa Indonesia tidak punya bentuk participle yang setara — biasanya diterjemahkan dengan kata sambung penuh ("Karena dia kehilangan paspornya..."), jadi user sering melewatkan reduced form ini sama sekali dan tetap memakai full clause.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Participle clauses banyak dipakai di narrative writing (travel blog, cerita pengalaman) untuk membuat tulisan terasa lebih matang dan tidak monoton dengan "because/who/which" berulang-ulang.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| itinerary /aɪˈtɪnərəri/ | a planned route or schedule for a trip | — |
| layover /ˈleɪoʊvər/ | a short stop between flights | — |
| customs (officer) /ˈkʌstəmz/ | the border checkpoint where goods/documents are inspected | Bukan "kebiasaan" — di sini artinya bea cukai |
| etiquette /ˈɛtɪkɪt/ | the accepted social behavior in a culture | — |
| disoriented /dɪsˈɔːrientɪd/ | confused about direction or surroundings | — |
| stranded /ˈstrændɪd/ | unable to leave a place due to circumstances | — |
| miscommunication /ˌmɪskəmjuːnɪˈkeɪʃən/ | a failure to communicate clearly, causing confusion | — |
| offend /əˈfɛnd/ | to upset or insult someone, often unintentionally | — |
| norm /nɔːrm/ | a standard or expected pattern of behavior | — |
| improvise /ˈɪmprəvaɪz/ | to make do with what's available without prior planning | — |
| get the hang of /ɡɛt ðə hæŋ ʌv/ | to learn how to do something after practice | — |
| run into (trouble) /rʌn ˈɪntuː/ | to unexpectedly encounter a problem | — |
| brush up on /brʌʃ ʌp ɒn/ | to quickly review or improve a skill | — |
| culture shock /ˈkʌltʃər ʃɒk/ | the disorientation felt when experiencing an unfamiliar culture | — |
| blend in /blɛnd ɪn/ | to not stand out, to look similar to the local environment | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: tidak menggunakan reduced clause karena terbiasa kata sambung penuh).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 5 (dispute, compromise, grievance, escalate, mediate, confront, accountability, ultimatum, leverage, concede, stand one's ground, back down, come to terms with, iron out, breakthrough) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal kapan participle clause membuat tulisan lebih elegan vs kapan terasa dipaksakan/overused.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks travel/cultural misunderstanding.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "run into trouble", "get the hang of", "brush up on (a language)". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval participle clause (contoh: "Describe a confusing moment abroad. Try starting with 'Having...' or 'Confused by...'").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi cerita pengalaman travel user dengan tone humble — soroti bahwa participle clause memang butuh waktu untuk terasa natural, jadi setiap percobaan layak dihargai walau belum sempurna.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat participle clause secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke ritme kalimat — participle clause di awal kalimat biasanya diikuti pause singkat sebelum main clause.

#### 🔗 PROMPT — Day 6 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

```

Mode Kilat: Pilih 5 kata dari BOW, 1 kalimat per kata.
(a) deskripsi singkat (b) contoh pakai KATA SAMA dari BOW (c) template latihan kosong.

### DAY 7 — Career Pivots & Professional Reinvention
**Grammar Focus:** Future Perfect & Future Continuous
🌉 *Overlap topic: Career sudah muncul di A2/B1 — di B2, fokusnya bergeser dari basic job-talk ke proyeksi jangka panjang dan reinvention karier.*

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Career pivots — pindah jalur karier, reinvention profesional, dan proyeksi jangka panjang tentang akan jadi apa seseorang di masa depan.

**Grammar Pendukung — Future Perfect & Future Continuous**

Day 7 memperkenalkan dua bentuk future yang sering tertukar: **Future Perfect** (aksi yang akan SELESAI sebelum titik waktu tertentu di masa depan) dan **Future Continuous** (aksi yang akan SEDANG BERLANGSUNG pada titik waktu tertentu di masa depan).

Pola:
- **Future Perfect:** Subject + will have + Past Participle — By next year, I will have finished my certification.
- **Future Continuous:** Subject + will be + V-ing — This time next month, she will be working at her new company.

Contoh kontras: "By 2027, I will have completed my MBA" (selesai sebelum 2027) vs "In 2027, I will be studying for my MBA" (masih berlangsung saat itu).

**Kontras dengan Day 6 (Participle Clauses):** Day 6 fokus ke meringkas dua clause jadi satu untuk narasi yang lebih ringkas. Day 7 fokus ke presisi waktu di masa depan — membedakan "akan selesai" vs "akan sedang berlangsung". Error umum: user memakai Future Simple biasa ("I will finish by next year") padahal konteksnya menuntut presisi completion-before-deadline (Future Perfect), atau salah pilih antara Future Perfect dan Future Continuous karena keduanya terdengar "akan" dalam Bahasa Indonesia.

**Catatan:** Bahasa Indonesia tidak membedakan "akan selesai sebelum X" dan "akan sedang berlangsung saat X" secara morfologis — keduanya sering hanya diterjemahkan "akan", jadi user perlu dilatih khusus mengenali signal kata seperti "by the time", "by next year" (→ Future Perfect) vs "at this time next year", "this time next month" (→ Future Continuous).

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Future Perfect/Continuous sering dipakai saat membahas career milestones, rencana jangka panjang dalam interview kerja, atau goal-setting profesional ("Where do you see yourself in 5 years?").

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| pivot (verb) /ˈpɪvət/ | to change direction or approach significantly | — |
| transferable (skills) /trænsˈfɜːrəbəl/ | skills that apply across different jobs or industries | — |
| burnout /ˈbɜːrnaʊt/ | extreme exhaustion from prolonged work stress | — |
| reinvent /ˌriːɪnˈvɛnt/ | to change oneself or one's career dramatically | — |
| credential /krəˈdɛnʃəl/ | a qualification or certification proving competence | — |
| networking /ˈnɛtwɜːrkɪŋ/ | building professional relationships and connections | — |
| severance (package) /ˈsɛvərəns/ | compensation given when someone leaves a job | — |
| fulfilling /fʊlˈfɪlɪŋ/ | giving a deep sense of satisfaction | — |
| stagnant /ˈstæɡnənt/ | not growing or progressing | — |
| freelance /ˈfriːlæns/ | working independently rather than for one employer | — |
| take the plunge /teɪk ðə plʌndʒ/ | to commit to a risky or significant decision | — |
| climb the ladder /klaɪm ðə ˈlædər/ | to advance through ranks in a career | — |
| step down (from) /stɛp daʊn/ | to resign or leave a position voluntarily | — |
| branch out (into) /bræntʃ aʊt/ | to expand into a new area or field | — |
| make ends meet /meɪk ɛndz miːt/ | to earn just enough money to cover basic needs | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: salah pilih Future Perfect vs Future Continuous karena keduanya "akan" di Bahasa Indonesia).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 6 (itinerary, layover, customs officer, etiquette, disoriented, stranded, miscommunication, offend, norm, improvise, get the hang of, run into trouble, brush up on, culture shock, blend in) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal kapan harus memilih antara Future Perfect dan Future Continuous berdasarkan signal kata waktu.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks career pivot.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "take the plunge", "climb the ladder", "branch out into (a new field)". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval Future Perfect/Continuous (contoh: "By this time next year, what will you have achieved in your career?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi refleksi karier user dengan tone humble — soroti bahwa membedakan Future Perfect dan Future Continuous memang butuh latihan berulang, jadi kesalahan di tahap ini normal dan bagian dari proses.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat Future Perfect dan Future Continuous secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke perbedaan stress pattern "will have + V3" vs "will be + V-ing".

### DAY 8 — Lifelong Learning & Alternative Education Paths
**Grammar Focus:** Wish/If Only + Would (complaints)
🌉 *Overlap topic: Education sudah muncul di A1/B1 — di B2, fokusnya bergeser dari basic school-talk ke lifelong learning dan jalur pendidikan alternatif (bootcamp, self-taught, online courses).*

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Lifelong learning, alternative education paths (bootcamp, online courses, self-taught skills) sebagai alternatif dari jalur pendidikan formal tradisional.

**Grammar Pendukung — Wish/If Only + Would (complaints)**

Day 8 memperkenalkan pola Wish/If Only + Would, khusus dipakai untuk mengekspresikan **complaint/keluhan** tentang kebiasaan orang lain (atau sesuatu) yang tidak mau berubah — beda dari wish biasa yang menyesali keadaan diri sendiri.

Pola: **I wish/If only + subject + would + bare infinitive** (subject HARUS berbeda dari "I" — tidak bisa "I wish I would...")

- I wish my university would update its outdated curriculum.
- If only more schools would offer flexible online options.
- I wish employers would value self-taught skills as much as formal degrees.

Kontras dengan wish biasa (regret): "I wish I had studied coding earlier" (Past Perfect, regret pribadi) vs "I wish my mentor would give clearer feedback" (would, complaint tentang orang lain).

**Kontras dengan Day 7 (Future Perfect & Future Continuous):** Day 7 fokus ke presisi proyeksi waktu di masa depan. Day 8 fokus ke ekspresi emosi — ketidakpuasan terhadap sesuatu yang tidak berubah, bukan soal waktu. Error umum: user memakai "I wish I would..." padahal subject wish dan would tidak boleh sama, atau memakai would untuk menyesali keadaan diri sendiri padahal seharusnya pakai Past Perfect (I wish I had... bukan I wish I would have...).

**Catatan:** Dalam Bahasa Indonesia, "saya berharap dia mau berubah" terdengar netral, tapi dalam English "I wish he would change" punya nuansa frustrasi/complaint yang kuat — user perlu disadarkan bahwa struktur ini bukan sekadar "harapan polos".

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Pola ini sering dipakai saat membahas sistem pendidikan yang dirasa kurang ideal, atau keluhan terhadap institusi/orang yang tidak kunjung berubah — relevan banget untuk topik lifelong learning yang sering melibatkan kritik terhadap pendidikan formal.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| self-taught /sɛlf tɔːt/ | having learned a skill without formal instruction | — |
| curriculum /kəˈrɪkjʊləm/ | the subjects and content taught in an educational program | — |
| outdated /aʊtˈdeɪtɪd/ | no longer current or relevant | — |
| credible /ˈkrɛdəbəl/ | believable and trustworthy | — |
| accreditation /əˌkrɛdɪˈteɪʃən/ | official recognition that a program meets certain standards | — |
| hands-on /hændz ɒn/ | involving direct practical experience rather than theory | — |
| stagnate /ˈstæɡneɪt/ | to stop developing or progressing | — |
| upskill /ʌpˈskɪl/ | to learn new or advanced skills | — |
| mentor /ˈmɛntɔːr/ | an experienced person who guides someone less experienced | — |
| credential inflation /krəˈdɛnʃəl ɪnˈfleɪʃən/ | the trend of requiring higher qualifications than necessary | — |
| keep up with /kiːp ʌp wɪð/ | to stay current with developments | — |
| fall behind /fɔːl bɪˈhaɪnd/ | to fail to progress at the same pace as others | — |
| invest in (oneself) /ɪnˈvɛst ɪn/ | to spend time/money to improve one's own future | — |
| outweigh /aʊtˈweɪ/ | to be more significant than something else | — |
| at one's own pace /æt wʌnz oʊn peɪs/ | progressing according to one's own preferred speed | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: memakai "I wish I would..." padahal subject harus berbeda).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 7 (pivot, transferable skills, burnout, reinvent, credential, networking, severance package, fulfilling, stagnant, freelance, take the plunge, climb the ladder, step down from, branch out into, make ends meet) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal nuansa emosional wish+would (complaint) vs wish+Past Perfect (regret).

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks lifelong learning.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "keep up with (the latest trends)", "invest in oneself", "at one's own pace". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval wish+would complaint (contoh: "What's one thing you wish your school or workplace would change about how they handle learning?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi keterbukaan user membahas frustrasi soal sistem pendidikan — tone humble, akui bahwa nuansa emosional wish+would memang halus dan butuh latihan untuk membedakannya dari sekadar harapan netral.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat wish/if only + would secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke nada suara yang menyiratkan sedikit frustrasi/keluhan, bukan sekadar harapan datar.

Feedback: kalimat lebih baik (B2) + penjelasan singkat English. Error B2 grammar -> bentuk benar dalam kurung italic.
"clue" -> petunjuk grammar saja. Lancar -> tambah 1 pertanyaan. Macet -> contoh + pattern drill.
Pujian singkat hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan tidak berlebihan.
```

### DAY 9 — Mental Health & Emotional Wellbeing
**Grammar Focus:** Modals of Speculation (Advanced)
🌉 *Overlap topic: Health sudah muncul di A1/A2/B1 — di B2, fokusnya bergeser dari physical health ke mental health/emotional wellbeing, dengan speculation tentang penyebab/kondisi yang lebih nuanced.*

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Mental health, emotional wellbeing, dan cara berspekulasi secara nuanced tentang kondisi psikologis diri sendiri atau orang lain — tanpa terdengar menuduh atau menyimpulkan secara pasti.

**Grammar Pendukung — Modals of Speculation (Advanced)**

Day 9 mengembangkan modals of deduction yang sudah dikenal di level sebelumnya (must be, might be, can't be) ke bentuk **advanced/perfect**, untuk berspekulasi tentang kondisi di MASA LALU.

Pola: **Modal + have + Past Participle**

- She must have been under a lot of stress lately. (deduksi kuat, masa lalu)
- He might have been dealing with anxiety without realizing it. (kemungkinan, masa lalu)
- They can't have known how serious it was. (deduksi negatif kuat, masa lalu)
- I could have handled that conversation better. (kemungkinan/regret, masa lalu)

**Kontras dengan Day 8 (Wish/If Only + Would):** Day 8 fokus ke complaint tentang sesuatu yang tidak mau berubah. Day 9 fokus ke spekulasi terukur tentang sebab/kondisi psikologis di masa lalu — bukan complaint, tapi educated guess yang empatik. Error umum: user memakai modal+V3 langsung tanpa "have" (salah: "must been stressed", benar: "must have been stressed"), atau memakai "must" untuk speculation ringan padahal seharusnya "might/could" (must terlalu kuat/pasti untuk topik sensitif seperti mental health).

**Catatan:** Dalam Bahasa Indonesia, "pasti dia stress" dan "mungkin dia stress" punya pembeda kata yang jelas (pasti vs mungkin), tapi user kadang lupa menyesuaikan kekuatan modal (must vs might vs could) dengan tingkat kepastian yang sebenarnya ingin disampaikan — terutama penting di topik sensitif seperti mental health supaya tidak terdengar menuduh.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Modal speculation advanced ini krusial untuk membahas mental health dengan empati — menebak kondisi psikologis seseorang tanpa terdengar menghakimi atau pasti ("must have been" terdengar lebih definitif dibanding "might have been" yang lebih hati-hati/sensitif).

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| overwhelmed /ˌoʊvərˈwɛlmd/ | feeling unable to cope with too much pressure | — |
| cope (with) /koʊp/ | to manage a difficult situation effectively | — |
| resilience /rɪˈzɪliəns/ | the ability to recover from difficulties | — |
| vulnerable /ˈvʌlnərəbəl/ | emotionally exposed or easily affected | — |
| therapy /ˈθɛrəpi/ | professional treatment for mental/emotional issues | — |
| stigma /ˈstɪɡmə/ | a negative judgment associated with a condition | — |
| self-care /sɛlf kɛr/ | activities done to maintain one's wellbeing | — |
| anxiety /æŋˈzaɪəti/ | a persistent feeling of worry or unease | — |
| isolation /ˌaɪsəˈleɪʃən/ | the state of being separated from others | — |
| acknowledge (feelings) /əkˈnɒlɪdʒ/ | to recognize someone's feelings as legitimate | — |
| bottle up /ˈbɒtəl ʌp/ | to suppress emotions instead of expressing them | — |
| open up (to someone) /ˈoʊpən ʌp/ | to share personal feelings honestly | — |
| take a toll (on) /teɪk ə toʊl/ | to cause gradual harm or damage | — |
| seek help /siːk hɛlp/ | to actively look for support or assistance | — |
| reach out (to someone) /riːtʃ aʊt/ | to make an effort to contact or support someone | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: lupa "have" setelah modal dalam speculation tentang masa lalu).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 8 (self-taught, curriculum, outdated, credible, accreditation, hands-on, stagnate, upskill, mentor, credential inflation, keep up with, fall behind, invest in oneself, outweigh, at one's own pace) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal memilih kekuatan modal (must/might/could) yang sesuai dengan sensitivitas topik mental health.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks mental health/wellbeing.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "take a toll on (someone)", "reach out to (someone)", "bottle up (emotions)". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval modal speculation advanced (contoh: "Think of a time a friend seemed off. What might have been going on?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara merespons topik mental health dengan extra kehati-hatian dan empati, tone humble dan tidak menggurui — apresiasi keterbukaan user membahas topik yang personal/sensitif, dan ingatkan secara halus bahwa AI ini bukan pengganti professional therapy jika konteksnya mengarah ke situasi serius.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat modal speculation advanced secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke nada suara yang hati-hati/empatik saat mengucapkan "might have been" vs nada lebih yakin untuk "must have been".

#### 🔗 PROMPT — Day 9 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

### DAY 10 — Artificial Intelligence & Its Impact on Daily Life
**Grammar Focus:** Future Forms (be about to / be due to / on the verge of)

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Artificial Intelligence dan dampaknya pada kehidupan sehari-hari — pekerjaan, privasi, kreativitas, dan bagaimana teknologi ini terus berkembang.

**Grammar Pendukung — Future Forms (be about to / be due to / on the verge of)**

Day 10 melengkapi rangkaian future forms B2 dengan tiga ekspresi yang menunjukkan derajat kepastian dan kedekatan waktu berbeda untuk hal yang akan terjadi di masa depan dekat.

Pola:
- **be about to + bare infinitive** (akan terjadi sangat segera): AI is about to transform how we work.
- **be due to + bare infinitive** (terjadwal/diperkirakan terjadi): The new AI regulation is due to take effect next year.
- **be on the verge of + gerund** (di ambang terjadi, sering perubahan besar): Many industries are on the verge of being completely automated.

**Kontras dengan Day 9 (Modals of Speculation Advanced):** Day 9 fokus ke spekulasi tentang kondisi/sebab di MASA LALU. Day 10 fokus ke kepastian/kedekatan suatu peristiwa di MASA DEPAN DEKAT — arah waktu yang berlawanan. Error umum: user memakai "be about to" untuk sesuatu yang masih jauh di masa depan (salah konteks — about to khusus untuk sangat segera), atau salah bentuk setelah "on the verge of" (harus gerund, bukan bare infinitive: salah "on the verge of break", benar "on the verge of breaking").

**Catatan:** Bahasa Indonesia punya "akan segera" yang bisa diterjemahkan ke ketiga ekspresi ini tanpa pembeda jelas, jadi user perlu dilatih mengenali nuansa: about to (sangat segera, momen ini), due to (terjadwal/expected), on the verge of (di ambang perubahan besar).

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Ketiga future forms ini sangat umum dipakai dalam diskusi tentang teknologi dan AI — artikel berita teknologi sering memakai "is due to launch", "is about to disrupt", "is on the verge of a breakthrough".

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| automation /ˌɔːtəˈmeɪʃən/ | the use of technology to perform tasks without human input | — |
| algorithm /ˈælɡərɪðəm/ | a set of rules a computer follows to solve a problem | — |
| disrupt /dɪsˈrʌpt/ | to fundamentally change an established system or industry | — |
| obsolete /ˌɒbsəˈliːt/ | no longer used because something newer has replaced it | — |
| iterate /ˈɪtəreɪt/ | to repeat a process with refinements each time | — |
| privacy concern /ˈpraɪvəsi kənˈsɜːrn/ | worry about personal data being misused or exposed | — |
| streamline /ˈstriːmlaɪn/ | to make a process simpler and more efficient | — |
| dependency /dɪˈpɛndənsi/ | reliance on something, sometimes excessively | — |
| ethical (concerns) /ˈɛθɪkəl/ | relating to moral principles | — |
| bias (in AI) /ˈbaɪəs/ | unfair distortion in AI outcomes, often from skewed data | — |
| augment /ɔːɡˈmɛnt/ | to enhance or add to something's capability | — |
| keep pace with /kiːp peɪs wɪð/ | to advance at the same speed as something else | — |
| phase out /feɪz aʊt/ | to gradually stop using or remove something | — |
| take over (a task) /teɪk ˈoʊvər/ | to assume control of something previously done by someone else | — |
| rely on /rɪˈlaɪ ɒn/ | to depend on someone or something | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: salah bentuk gerund setelah "on the verge of").

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 9 (overwhelmed, cope with, resilience, vulnerable, therapy, stigma, self-care, anxiety, isolation, acknowledge feelings, bottle up, open up to someone, take a toll on, seek help, reach out to someone) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal nuansa kepastian/kedekatan waktu (about to vs due to vs on the verge of).

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks AI/teknologi.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "keep pace with (technology)", "phase out (old systems)", "rely on (AI tools)". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval future forms (contoh: "What industry do you think is on the verge of being completely transformed by AI?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi sudut pandang user soal AI dengan tone humble — soroti progress user dari Day 3 sampai Day 10 dalam menguasai berbagai future forms yang sudah dipelajari (Future Perfect/Continuous di Day 7, sekarang be about to/due to/on the verge of), tanpa menggurui.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat be about to / be due to / on the verge of secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke pelafalan natural frasa-frasa ini dalam kalimat cepat, sebagaimana sering muncul di percakapan informal tentang tren teknologi.

### DAY 11 — City Life & Urban Planning
**Grammar Focus:** Passive Voice with Gerund & Infinitive

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** City life, urban planning, dan tantangan kota besar — zonasi, infrastruktur, dan proyek revitalisasi yang mengubah wajah kota.

**Grammar Pendukung — Passive Voice with Gerund & Infinitive**

Day 11 menggabungkan Passive Voice dengan bentuk non-finite — gerund (-ing) dan infinitive (to + V) — yang sering muncul setelah verb tertentu seperti need, dislike, expect, deserve.

Pola:
- **need + V-ing (passive meaning) = need + to be + V3:** This road needs widening. = This road needs to be widened.
- **dislike/hate/love + being + V3:** Residents dislike being relocated without proper notice.
- **expect/deserve + to be + V3:** This neighborhood deserves to be redeveloped responsibly.

**Kontras dengan Day 10 (Future Forms):** Day 10 fokus ke kepastian/kedekatan waktu suatu peristiwa di masa depan (about to/due to/on the verge of). Day 11 fokus ke kombinasi passive voice dengan bentuk non-finite setelah verb tertentu — bukan soal waktu, tapi soal struktur kalimat yang menyiratkan makna pasif tanpa "be + V3" penuh. Error umum: user memakai gerund/infinitive aktif padahal maknanya pasif (salah: "This road needs to repair", benar: "This road needs to be repaired" atau "needs repairing"), atau lupa "being" sebelum V3 setelah dislike/enjoy.

**Catatan:** Bahasa Indonesia tidak punya pembeda morfologis antara "perlu diperbaiki" (pasif) dan "perlu memperbaiki" (aktif) yang konsisten dengan struktur ini, jadi user sering memakai infinitive aktif ("needs to repair") padahal jalan itu yang seharusnya diperbaiki, bukan jalan yang memperbaiki sesuatu.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Struktur ini sangat umum dalam diskusi urban planning — laporan kota, proposal renovasi infrastruktur, atau keluhan warga tentang fasilitas publik yang butuh perbaikan.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| zoning /ˈzoʊnɪŋ/ | the division of a city into areas for specific uses | — |
| congestion /kənˈdʒɛstʃən/ | overcrowding, especially of traffic | — |
| gentrification /ˌdʒɛntrɪfɪˈkeɪʃən/ | the process of an area becoming wealthier, often displacing residents | — |
| infrastructure /ˈɪnfrəstrʌktʃər/ | the basic physical systems of a city (roads, utilities, etc.) | — |
| urban sprawl /ˈɜːrbən sprɔːl/ | the uncontrolled expansion of a city into surrounding areas | — |
| pedestrian-friendly /pəˈdɛstriən frɛndli/ | designed to be safe and convenient for people walking | — |
| revitalize /riːˈvaɪtəlaɪz/ | to bring new life or energy to a declining area | — |
| displacement /dɪsˈpleɪsmənt/ | being forced to move from one's home or area | — |
| accessibility /əkˌsɛsəˈbɪləti/ | the quality of being easy to reach or use for everyone | — |
| encroach (on) /ɪnˈkroʊtʃ/ | to gradually intrude on land or space | — |
| overcrowded /ˌoʊvərˈkraʊdɪd/ | containing too many people for the available space | — |
| bottleneck /ˈbɒtəlnɛk/ | a point of congestion that slows down a whole system | — |
| high-rise /haɪ raɪz/ | a tall building with many floors | — |
| redevelop /ˌriːdɪˈvɛləp/ | to rebuild or transform an area for a new purpose | — |
| relocate /ˌriːloʊˈkeɪt/ | to move to a different place | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: memakai infinitive aktif padahal maknanya pasif, seperti "needs to repair" alih-alih "needs to be repaired").

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 10 (automation, algorithm, disrupt, obsolete, iterate, privacy concern, streamline, dependency, ethical concerns, bias in AI, augment, keep pace with, phase out, take over a task, rely on) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal kapan memilih gerund vs infinitive setelah verb tertentu (need, deserve, dislike).

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks urban planning.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "ease congestion", "encroach on (green space)", "in need of redevelopment". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval passive+gerund/infinitive (contoh: "What part of your city needs improving the most, and why does it deserve to be prioritized?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi observasi user tentang kota tempat tinggalnya dengan tone humble — soroti bahwa membedakan gerund vs infinitive setelah verb tertentu memang butuh eksposur berulang, jadi kesalahan kecil di tahap ini normal.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat passive+gerund/infinitive secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke pengucapan natural "needs -ing" vs "needs to be + V3" dalam kalimat spontan.

#### 🔗 PROMPT — Day 11 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

### DAY 12 — The Justice System & Fair Trials
**Grammar Focus:** Subjunctive in Formal Contexts

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** The justice system, fair trials, dan proses hukum formal — dari sidang pengadilan sampai keputusan akhir hakim.

**Grammar Pendukung — Subjunctive in Formal Contexts**

Day 12 mengembangkan subjunctive yang sudah dikenal di Day 5 (insist/recommend/suggest) ke konteks formal/legal yang lebih luas: "it is + adjective + that" dan verb formal seperti demand, require, propose.

Pola:
- **It is + adjective (essential/vital/crucial) + that + subject + bare infinitive:** It is essential that the defendant be present at the hearing.
- **demand/require/propose + that + subject + bare infinitive:** The court demanded that the witness testify under oath.

Contoh lengkap:
- It is crucial that justice be served fairly.
- The judge proposed that the case be reviewed further.
- The law requires that all evidence be disclosed before trial.

**Kontras dengan Day 11 (Passive Voice with Gerund & Infinitive):** Day 11 fokus ke kombinasi passive dengan bentuk non-finite setelah verb tertentu (need, dislike, expect). Day 12 fokus ke subjunctive formal — bare infinitive yang dipicu oleh adjective evaluatif ("it is essential that...") atau verb mandative (demand, require, propose) dalam konteks hukum yang sangat formal. Error umum: user mengonjugasikan verb seperti biasa (salah: "it is essential that he is present", benar: "it is essential that he be present"), atau menambahkan "should" yang sebenarnya boleh tapi lebih British/kurang formal dibanding bare subjunctive.

**Catatan:** Mirip dengan Day 5, subjunctive ini tidak punya bentuk setara persis di Bahasa Indonesia — "penting bahwa dia hadir" tidak menuntut perubahan bentuk kata kerja seperti di English, jadi user sering lupa bahwa subjunctive di sini HARUS bare infinitive (tanpa -s, tanpa "is/are/was/were").

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Subjunctive formal ini sangat umum di dokumen hukum, putusan pengadilan, kontrak, dan diskusi formal tentang sistem keadilan — termasuk debat tentang reformasi hukum.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| verdict /ˈvɜːrdɪkt/ | the formal decision made by a jury or judge | — |
| testimony /ˈtɛstɪməni/ | a formal statement given as evidence in court | — |
| defendant /dɪˈfɛndənt/ | the person accused in a court case | — |
| plaintiff /ˈpleɪntɪf/ | the person who brings a case against another in court | — |
| acquit /əˈkwɪt/ | to formally declare someone not guilty | — |
| prosecute /ˈprɒsɪkjuːt/ | to bring legal action against someone in court | — |
| allegation /ˌælɪˈɡeɪʃən/ | a claim that someone has done something wrong, not yet proven | — |
| witness /ˈwɪtnəs/ | a person who gives evidence in court | — |
| jury /ˈdʒʊri/ | a group of citizens who decide a verdict in a trial | — |
| unanimous /juːˈnænɪməs/ | with everyone in full agreement | — |
| uphold (a ruling) /ʌpˈhoʊld/ | to confirm or maintain a previous legal decision | — |
| overturn (a verdict) /ˌoʊvərˈtɜːrn/ | to officially reverse a previous decision | — |
| miscarriage of justice /mɪsˈkærɪdʒ ʌv ˈdʒʌstɪs/ | a wrongful conviction or unfair legal outcome | — |
| beyond reasonable doubt /bɪˈjɒnd ˈriːzənəbəl daʊt/ | the legal standard of certainty needed to convict | — |
| sentencing /ˈsɛntənsɪŋ/ | the process of deciding a punishment for a convicted person | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: mengonjugasikan verb setelah subjunctive trigger padahal harus bare infinitive).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 11 (zoning, congestion, gentrification, infrastructure, urban sprawl, pedestrian-friendly, revitalize, displacement, accessibility, encroach on, overcrowded, bottleneck, high-rise, redevelop, relocate) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal register formal yang dituntut oleh subjunctive dalam konteks hukum.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks sistem hukum.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "beyond reasonable doubt", "uphold a ruling", "miscarriage of justice". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval subjunctive formal (contoh: "Why is it essential that a jury reach a unanimous decision in serious cases?").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi usaha user menulis dengan register formal yang dituntut topik hukum — tone humble, akui bahwa subjunctive formal memang salah satu struktur yang jarang dipakai di percakapan sehari-hari sehingga butuh latihan ekstra.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat subjunctive formal secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke nada formal/tegas yang biasanya menyertai kalimat seperti "It is essential that..." dalam konteks hukum.

### DAY 13 — Marketing Tricks & Consumer Psychology
**Grammar Focus:** Cleft Sentences for Emphasis

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Marketing tricks, consumer psychology, dan cara brand memanfaatkan psikologi manusia untuk mendorong keputusan membeli.

**Grammar Pendukung — Cleft Sentences for Emphasis**

Day 13 memperkenalkan Cleft Sentences — struktur yang "membelah" kalimat sederhana menjadi dua bagian untuk memberi emphasis pada elemen tertentu.

Pola:
- **It-cleft:** It + be + [emphasized element] + that/who + rest of sentence — It is the packaging that influences buyers the most.
- **Wh-cleft (pseudo-cleft):** What/Who + rest of sentence + be + [emphasized element] — What really drives sales is scarcity. / What consumers want is authenticity.

Contoh lengkap:
- It was the discount that convinced her to buy immediately.
- It is brand loyalty, not price, that keeps customers coming back.
- What surprises most people is how easily they're influenced by color psychology.

**Kontras dengan Day 12 (Subjunctive in Formal Contexts):** Day 12 fokus ke struktur formal/legal untuk mandat (it is essential that...). Day 13 fokus ke emphasis — menonjolkan elemen tertentu dalam kalimat lewat restrukturisasi, bukan soal formalitas tapi soal penekanan. Error umum: user lupa relative pronoun di it-cleft (salah: "It is the price what...", benar: "It is the price that..."), atau salah agreement verb di wh-cleft.

**Catatan:** Bahasa Indonesia biasa memberi emphasis lewat intonasi atau partikel ("justru harga yang..."), bukan lewat restrukturisasi kalimat seperti English — jadi user sering melewatkan cleft sentence sama sekali dan tetap pakai kalimat biasa walau ingin menekankan sesuatu.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Cleft sentences sangat umum dalam analisis marketing dan iklan — artikel tentang consumer psychology sering memakai struktur ini untuk menonjolkan faktor penentu di balik keputusan membeli.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| scarcity /ˈskɛrsəti/ | the perception of limited availability, used to drive urgency | — |
| bandwagon effect /ˈbændwæɡən ɪˈfɛkt/ | the tendency to do something because others are doing it | — |
| impulsive (buying) /ɪmˈpʌlsɪv/ | acting suddenly without careful thought | — |
| subconscious /sʌbˈkɒnʃəs/ | part of the mind influencing behavior without awareness | — |
| persuasive /pərˈsweɪsɪv/ | effective at convincing someone | — |
| gimmick /ˈɡɪmɪk/ | a trick or device used to attract attention | — |
| brand loyalty /brænd ˈlɔɪəlti/ | a consumer's consistent preference for one brand | — |
| endorsement /ɪnˈdɔːrsmənt/ | public support for a product, often by a celebrity | — |
| target audience /ˈtɑːrɡɪt ˈɔːdiəns/ | the specific group a product is marketed to | — |
| manipulate /məˈnɪpjʊleɪt/ | to influence someone unfairly or deceptively | — |
| appeal to (emotions) /əˈpiːl tuː/ | to attract or interest someone's feelings | — |
| capitalize on /ˈkæpɪtəlaɪz ɒn/ | to take advantage of a situation for benefit | — |
| stand out (from competitors) /stænd aʊt/ | to be noticeably different or better | — |
| word of mouth /wɜːrd ʌv maʊθ/ | information spread by people talking to each other | — |
| susceptible (to) /səˈsɛptəbəl/ | easily influenced or affected by something | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: lupa relative pronoun "that" di it-cleft).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 12 (verdict, testimony, defendant, plaintiff, acquit, prosecute, allegation, witness, jury, unanimous, uphold a ruling, overturn a verdict, miscarriage of justice, beyond reasonable doubt, sentencing) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal kapan it-cleft vs wh-cleft terdengar lebih natural sesuai konteks.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks marketing/consumer psychology.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "capitalize on (a trend)", "appeal to (emotions)", "stand out from competitors". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval cleft sentence (contoh: "What is it that makes you trust one brand over another? Try starting with 'What really matters to me is...' or 'It is... that...'").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi analisis user tentang trik marketing yang pernah dialami sendiri — tone humble, soroti bahwa cleft sentence memang struktur yang jarang diajarkan eksplisit, jadi progress sekecil apapun di sini layak diapresiasi.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat cleft sentence secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke stress/penekanan pada elemen yang di-emphasize, sesuai fungsi cleft sentence itu sendiri.

### DAY 14 — Globalization & Cultural Exchange
**Grammar Focus:** Advanced Linking & Discourse Markers

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Globalisasi dan pertukaran budaya — bagaimana budaya saling mempengaruhi, berasimilasi, atau justru tergerus akibat interaksi global.

**Grammar Pendukung — Advanced Linking & Discourse Markers**

Day 14 memperkenalkan discourse markers tingkat akademik untuk menghubungkan ide secara lebih presisi daripada konektor dasar (but, so, also).

Pola & contoh:
- **whereas** (kontras) — Some cultures embrace fusion, whereas others resist outside influence.
- **insofar as** (sejauh) — The policy succeeded insofar as it preserved local traditions.
- **in light of** (mengingat) — In light of rising globalization, many communities are reviving traditional practices.
- **with regard to** (terkait dengan) — With regard to cultural appropriation, opinions remain divided.
- **as opposed to** (berbeda dengan) — They chose integration as opposed to isolation.
- **conversely** (sebaliknya) — Some traditions fade with globalization; conversely, others gain global popularity.

**Kontras dengan Day 13 (Cleft Sentences for Emphasis):** Day 13 fokus ke restrukturisasi kalimat untuk emphasis. Day 14 fokus ke discourse markers — kata/frasa penghubung yang mengatur logika antar-klausa atau antar-kalimat secara akademik, bukan soal penekanan tapi soal presisi hubungan logis (kontras, kondisi, referensi).

**Catatan:** Discourse markers ini murni elemen grammar/struktur kalimat, bukan kosakata topik — jadi TIDAK dimasukkan ke tabel BOW (BOW khusus untuk vocabulary tematik). Latihan penggunaannya akan muncul di Langkah 5 (Transition Words) dan dalam contoh kalimat Grammar Pendukung ini.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Discourse markers seperti ini umum dalam esai akademik, artikel opini, dan diskusi formal tentang isu lintas budaya — penting untuk level B2 yang mulai menulis argumentasi kompleks.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| globalization /ˌɡləʊbəlaɪˈzeɪʃən/ | the process of increasing interconnection between countries | — |
| diaspora /daɪˈæspərə/ | a population living outside its original homeland | — |
| fusion /ˈfjuːʒən/ | a blend of different cultural elements | — |
| heritage /ˈhɛrɪtɪdʒ/ | traditions and values passed down through generations | — |
| appropriation /əˌprəʊpriˈeɪʃən/ | taking elements of another culture, often controversially | — |
| homogenize /həˈmɒdʒənaɪz/ | to make uniform, removing differences | — |
| assimilate /əˈsɪmɪleɪt/ | to adopt the customs of a new culture | — |
| erode (traditions) /ɪˈrəʊd/ | to gradually wear away or weaken | — |
| preserve /prɪˈzɜːv/ | to keep something unchanged or protected | — |
| integrate /ˈɪntɪɡreɪt/ | to combine and become part of a larger whole | — |
| multicultural /ˌmʌltiˈkʌltʃərəl/ | involving several different cultures | — |
| indigenous /ɪnˈdɪdʒɪnəs/ | originating naturally in a particular place | — |
| interconnected /ˌɪntərkəˈnɛktɪd/ | linked together, mutually dependent | — |
| hybrid (identity) /ˈhaɪbrɪd/ | a combination of two or more distinct elements | — |
| give way to /ɡɪv weɪ tuː/ | to be replaced by something else | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: salah penempatan "whereas" di tengah kalimat tanpa koma).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 13 (scarcity, bandwagon effect, impulsive buying, subconscious, persuasive, gimmick, brand loyalty, endorsement, target audience, manipulate, appeal to emotions, capitalize on, stand out from competitors, word of mouth, susceptible to) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal variasi discourse markers agar tidak repetitif.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, menggunakan minimal 2 discourse markers dari Grammar Pendukung.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: whereas, insofar as, in light of, with regard to, as opposed to, conversely + contoh English relevan ke konteks globalisasi/budaya.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "preserve (cultural) heritage", "give way to (modern trends)", "erode traditions". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval discourse marker (contoh: "How has globalization affected your local traditions? Try using 'whereas' or 'conversely' to contrast two views.").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi sudut pandang personal user soal budaya — tone humble, soroti bahwa discourse markers seperti ini butuh waktu untuk terasa natural, jadi setiap percobaan layak diapresiasi tanpa menggurui.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat dengan discourse markers secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke kejelasan hubungan logis antar-ide, bukan sekadar pengucapan kata.

### DAY 15 — Changing Gender Roles in Society
**Grammar Focus:** Ellipsis & Substitution

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Perubahan peran gender dalam masyarakat — ekspektasi tradisional vs nilai-nilai egaliter modern.

**Grammar Pendukung — Ellipsis & Substitution**

Day 15 memperkenalkan Ellipsis (menghilangkan kata yang sudah jelas dari konteks) dan Substitution (mengganti kata/frasa dengan kata pengganti seperti "so", "one", "do") untuk menghindari pengulangan dalam tulisan natural.

Pola & contoh:
- **Ellipsis:** She wants to challenge traditional norms, and he does [want to challenge traditional norms] too → She wants to challenge traditional norms, and he does too.
- **Substitution (so):** "Is gender equality improving?" "I believe so." (so = that gender equality is improving)
- **Substitution (one/ones):** Traditional roles are fading; modern ones are taking their place.
- **Substitution (do/does/did):** He doesn't conform to stereotypes, but his brother does.

**Kontras dengan Day 14 (Advanced Linking & Discourse Markers):** Day 14 fokus ke konektor untuk menghubungkan ide secara eksplisit. Day 15 justru fokus ke ekonomi bahasa — menghilangkan atau mengganti elemen yang berulang agar tulisan tidak repetitif, kebalikan dari menambah penjelasan.

**Catatan:** Dalam Bahasa Indonesia, pengulangan kata sering tidak masalah ("Dia mau, aku juga mau"), sedangkan dalam English natural lebih sering memakai ellipsis/substitution ("She wants to, and I do too") — user perlu dilatih sadar akan kebiasaan repetisi yang terasa janggal di English.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Ellipsis dan substitution sangat umum dalam percakapan natural dan tulisan opini tentang isu sosial seperti gender roles, di mana perbandingan antar-kelompok (pria vs wanita, tradisional vs modern) sering muncul berulang.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| stereotype /ˈstɛriətaɪp/ | a fixed, oversimplified idea about a group of people | — |
| breadwinner /ˈbrɛdwɪnər/ | the main income earner in a household | — |
| caregiver /ˈkɛrɡɪvər/ | a person who looks after someone, often a family member | — |
| expectation (societal) /ˌɛkspɛkˈteɪʃən/ | a belief about how someone should behave | — |
| egalitarian /ɪˌɡælɪˈtɛəriən/ | believing in equal rights and opportunities for all | — |
| patriarchal /ˌpeɪtriˈɑːkəl/ | relating to a system dominated by men | — |
| empowerment /ɪmˈpaʊərmənt/ | the process of gaining confidence and control over one's life | — |
| double standard /ˈdʌbəl ˈstændərd/ | unfair application of different rules to similar groups | — |
| nurture /ˈnɜːtʃər/ | to care for and encourage the growth of someone | — |
| conform (to) /kənˈfɔːm/ | to behave according to accepted standards | — |
| challenge (norms) /ˈtʃælɪndʒ/ | to question or resist accepted standards | — |
| redefine /ˌriːdɪˈfaɪn/ | to define something again, usually differently | — |
| traditional (roles) /trəˈdɪʃənəl/ | following long-established customs or beliefs | — |
| inclusive /ɪnˈkluːsɪv/ | not excluding any group of people | — |
| defy (expectations) /dɪˈfaɪ/ | to openly resist or refuse to follow | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: mengulang kata kerja penuh padahal bisa pakai substitution "does too").

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 14 (globalization, diaspora, fusion, heritage, appropriation, homogenize, assimilate, erode traditions, preserve, integrate, multicultural, indigenous, interconnected, hybrid identity, give way to) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal kapan ellipsis/substitution membuat tulisan lebih natural vs kapan repetisi tetap perlu untuk kejelasan.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, menggunakan minimal 1 contoh ellipsis dan 1 contoh substitution.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: by and large, given that, provided that, notwithstanding, albeit, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks gender roles.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "challenge norms", "defy expectations", "redefine traditional roles". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for formal topics, or overly academic/stiff for conversational ones). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval substitution (contoh: "Do you think gender roles are changing in your community? Try answering with 'I believe so' or 'Some do, but others don't.'").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi keberanian user membahas topik sensitif seperti gender roles — tone humble, hindari menghakimi sudut pandang user, fokus pada kualitas bahasa bukan opini personalnya.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat dengan ellipsis/substitution secara lisan, dipicu trigger eksplisit dari Kak Ara. Fokus ke kelancaran menghindari pengulangan kata yang tidak perlu.

### DAY 16 — Taking Risks: How We Make Big Decisions
**Grammar Focus:** Verbs of Senses + Adjective/Gerund

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Mengambil risiko besar dalam hidup — keputusan karir, relasi, keuangan, atau hidup baru — dan apa yang mendorong atau menahan seseorang untuk melangkah.

**Grammar Pendukung — Verbs of Senses + Adjective/Gerund**

Day 16 memperkenalkan pola sense verbs yang diikuti oleh adjective atau gerund: feel/sound/look/seem/appear + adjective, serta feel/look like + gerund.

Pola & contoh:
- **Sense verb + adjective:** The decision feels irreversible. / The plan sounds risky. / She seemed hesitant to commit.
- **Sense verb + like + gerund:** It feels like giving up. / That sounds like taking a huge leap of faith.
- **Look/seem + adjective (describing state):** The outcome looked uncertain. / He seemed overwhelmed by the options.

Error umum: user sering menulis "it feels like risk" (noun) padahal idiomatically harus "it feels risky" (adj) atau "it feels like taking a risk" (gerund).

**Kontras dengan Day 15 (Ellipsis & Substitution):** Day 15 fokus ke *ekonomi bahasa* — menghilangkan kata yang berulang. Day 16 fokus ke *deskripsi persepsi* — bagaimana sesuatu terasa, terlihat, atau terdengar — menggunakan sense verbs yang diikuti adjective atau gerund, bukan noun.

**Catatan:** Dalam Bahasa Indonesia, kita sering memakai "terasa seperti risiko" (noun) — padahal English lebih natural dengan adjective: "it feels risky". Pola "feels like + gerund" juga tidak ada padanan langsung di Bahasa Indonesia.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Pola ini sangat umum dalam konteks personal reflection, journaling, dan percakapan tentang keputusan besar — bukan grammar formal/akademis, tapi justru terdengar sangat natural di level B2 ke atas.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| venture /ˈvɛntʃər/ | a risky or daring undertaking | — |
| threshold /ˈθrɛʃhoʊld/ | the point at which something begins or changes | — |
| leap of faith /liːp əv feɪθ/ | an act of trusting something without certainty | Catatan: bukan "lompatan kepercayaan" harfiah — idiom untuk keputusan berani tanpa jaminan |
| weigh up /weɪ ʌp/ | to carefully consider the pros and cons before deciding | — |
| intuition /ˌɪntjʊˈɪʃən/ | immediate understanding without conscious reasoning | — |
| commitment /kəˈmɪtmənt/ | a pledge or dedicated effort to follow through | — |
| irreversible /ˌɪrɪˈvɜːsɪbəl/ | impossible to undo or change back | — |
| overwhelming /ˌoʊvərˈwɛlmɪŋ/ | extremely intense or too much to manage | — |
| hesitate /ˈhɛzɪteɪt/ | to pause before acting because of uncertainty | — |
| uncertainty /ʌnˈsɜːtənti/ | the state of not knowing what will happen | — |
| come to terms with /kʌm tə tɜːmz wɪð/ | to gradually accept something difficult | Catatan: idiom — bukan "datang untuk berdamai" harfiah |
| gut feeling /ɡʌt ˈfiːlɪŋ/ | an instinctive reaction rather than logical reasoning | Catatan: bukan perasaan fisik di perut — artinya "insting" |
| ambitious /æmˈbɪʃəs/ | having a strong desire to achieve significant things | — |
| back out (of) /bæk aʊt/ | to withdraw from a commitment or plan | — |
| calculate /ˈkælkjʊleɪt/ | to assess carefully before making a decision | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: "it feels like risk" instead of "it feels risky" karena pola noun Bahasa Indonesia).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 15 (stereotype, breadwinner, caregiver, expectation (societal), egalitarian, patriarchal, empowerment, double standard, nurture, conform (to), challenge (norms), redefine, traditional (roles), inclusive, defy (expectations)) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal bagaimana native speakers C1+ menggunakan sense verbs untuk nuance emosional yang lebih kompleks dari sekedar "it seems good/bad".

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, gunakan minimal 2 sense verb + adjective/gerund secara natural.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks decision-making.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "weigh up the options", "take a leap of faith", "come to terms with uncertainty". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the topic's context (too casual for reflective/analytical tone, or overly stiff). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval sense verb + adjective/gerund (contoh: "Describe a big decision you made. How did it feel at the time? Start your answer with 'It felt...' or 'It seemed like...'").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi keberanian user membahas keputusan personal — tone humble, hindari menghakimi pilihan hidup user. Soroti kalau user sudah mulai memakai sense verbs secara natural, karena pola ini sering underused di level B1.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan kalimat dengan sense verbs secara lisan. Kak Ara meminta user mendeskripsikan keputusan terakhirnya menggunakan minimal 2 pola: "It felt...", "It seemed like...", atau "Looking back, it sounds...". Fokus ke kelancaran dan naturalness penggunaan adjective vs gerund.

#### 🔗 PROMPT — Day 16 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

```

Level bahasa Inggrisku: B2 (Upper-Intermediate).
Kamu Kak Ara dari Inggrisin Yuk, AI Coach. Bimbing aku vocab writing+speaking Level B2.

Bahasa: English dominan. "Catatan:" Indonesia max 1-2 poin interferensi. Emoji ok. Phonetic UK dalam / /.
LANGKAH 1 - SAPAAN+BOW+WRITING CHALLENGE (1 response):
Sapa English, tampilkan BOW+Writing Challenge. Jangan tanya "ready?".
BOW (PERSIS 15 kata ini, jangan ganti):
venture, threshold, leap of faith, weigh up, intuition, commitment, irreversible, overwhelming, hesitate, uncertainty, come to terms with, gut feeling, ambitious, back out (of), calculate
Tabel 3 kolom: Kosakata+phonetic UK | English definition | Catatan Indonesia ("-" default).

Mode Cerita: Write 7-9 sentences about a big decision you made or are considering. Min 5 kata dari BOW. Gunakan Verbs of Senses + Adj/Gerund (feels risky, sounds like giving up).
Mode Kilat: Pilih 5 kata dari BOW, 1 kalimat per kata.
(a) deskripsi singkat (b) contoh pakai KATA SAMA dari BOW (c) template latihan kosong.
Jangan bocorkan langkah koreksi - tunggu jawabanku.
LANGKAH 2 - KOREKSI 8 LANGKAH (otomatis setelah aku kirim tulisan):
1. Koreksi Writing - tabel 3 kolom: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat Benar | Why (English). Max 2 error utama. >=95% benar: OK. "Catatan:" max 1-2.
2. Analisa BOW - tiap kata: tepat/belum tepat + contoh English. Vocab Refresh: singgung 1-2 kata BOW Day sebelumnya.
3. Analisa CEFR - level saat ini + yang sudah bagus + 2 tips naik ke C1 (English).
4. 5W+1H - tabel English + "Enriched Paragraph": full English, no translation.
5. Transition Words - jika belum: 2-3 B2 connector (notwithstanding, albeit, given that, by and large) + contoh English.
6. Lexical Chunks - 2-3 collocations B2+ speakers use for topik ini. Format: chunk -> "example." (note). Sarankan 1 jika belum.
Kalau tulisanku kosong/off-topic/Indonesia: minta tulis 7-9 kalimat English dulu.
7. Register Check - 1-2 frasa register tidak cocok? Original -> Better -> Why (1 sentence English). OK jika konsisten.
8. Speaking Challenge - 3 pertanyaan English topik Taking Risks: How We Make Big Decisions (min 1 memicu retrieval grammar):
Describe a time you stood at a threshold - did it feel too overwhelming to move forward?
How do you weigh up an irreversible decision - do you trust your intuition or calculate the risks?
Has there been a venture you backed out of and later regretted? What made the uncertainty feel too great?
LANGKAH 3 - MODE SPEAKING (trigger: Let's start speaking!):
Ulangi Speaking Challenge satu per satu, English. Langsung, jangan basa-basi.
Transkrip jawabanku ke Inggris. Koreksi dalam English. Kalau stuck: boleh 1 clue Indonesia singkat.
Feedback: kalimat lebih baik (B2) + penjelasan singkat English. Error B2 grammar -> bentuk benar dalam kurung italic.
"clue" -> petunjuk grammar saja. Lancar -> tambah 1 pertanyaan. Macet -> contoh + pattern drill.
Pujian singkat hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan tidak berlebihan.
```
