### DAY 28 — The Future of Work & Automation 🌉
**Grammar Focus:** Future Forms Combo (Future Perfect + Continuous + Be About To)

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Masa depan pekerjaan di era otomasi — bagaimana AI dan robotik mengubah lanskap karir, siapa yang paling terdampak, dan apa artinya bagi keahlian yang perlu dimiliki generasi berikutnya.

> 🌉 **Bridge Day:** Future Forms Combo adalah C1 precision grammar — menggunakan tiga future forms secara tepat dalam satu narasi.

**Grammar Pendukung — Future Forms Combo**

Day 28 menggabungkan tiga future forms yang sudah diperkenalkan di Day 7 (Future Perfect/Continuous) dan Day 10 (Future Forms) dengan pola tambahan:

- **Future Perfect (will have + pp):** By 2035, automation will have replaced a significant percentage of routine jobs. / Once the transition is complete, millions of workers will have been forced to reskill entirely.
- **Future Continuous (will be + V-ing):** In ten years, more people will be working in roles that don't exist today. / Algorithms will be making an increasing share of hiring decisions.
- **Be about to / be due to / be on the verge of:** The gig economy is about to undergo a dramatic transformation. / The shift towards remote work is due to accelerate further. / Traditional white-collar roles are on the verge of being disrupted.

**Combo kalimat contoh:**
- By 2040, AI will have transformed nearly every white-collar profession, and most workers will be navigating hybrid roles that are currently on the verge of being created.
- The moment automation is about to make a job obsolete, workers who have been upskilling consistently will have positioned themselves for the next wave.

Error umum: user mencampur future continuous dan future perfect tanpa memperhatikan kapan masing-masing dipakai — future continuous untuk aksi yang *sedang terjadi* di masa depan; future perfect untuk aksi yang *sudah selesai* pada titik tertentu di masa depan.

**Kontras dengan Day 27 (Comparatives + Inversion):** Day 27 membandingkan keadaan yang sudah ada. Day 28 memproyeksikan perubahan ke masa depan dengan presisi temporal — tiga future forms memberikan nuance berbeda: progression (continuous), completion (perfect), dan imminence (about to).

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Future Forms Combo sangat umum dalam business forecasting, economic reports, dan career planning discussions — tanda tulisan analytical yang matang.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| automation /ˌɔːtəˈmeɪʃən/ | the use of machines and technology to perform tasks without humans | — |
| redundancy /rɪˈdʌndənsi/ | loss of a job because it is no longer needed by the employer | Catatan: dalam konteks pekerjaan, "redundancy" = PHK karena jabatan dihapus — bukan "berulang/tidak perlu" |
| reskill /riːˈskɪl/ | to learn new skills to qualify for a different type of work | — |
| gig economy /ɡɪɡ ɪˈkɒnəmi/ | an economy based on short-term, flexible employment contracts | — |
| disruptive /dɪsˈrʌptɪv/ | causing radical change to an established industry or system | — |
| on the verge of /ɒn ðə vɜːdʒ əv/ | very close to experiencing or doing something | — |
| upskill /ʌpˈskɪl/ | to improve or develop one's existing skills for better opportunities | — |
| hybrid work /ˈhaɪbrɪd wɜːk/ | a model combining remote and in-office working arrangements | — |
| obsolete /ˌɒbsəˈliːt/ | no longer useful or needed due to advancement or change | — |
| cognitive skill /ˈkɒɡnɪtɪv skɪl/ | a mental ability such as reasoning, problem-solving, or creativity | — |
| inevitably /ɪnˈɛvɪtəbli/ | in a way that cannot be avoided or prevented | — |
| blue-collar /ˈbluː ˈkɒlər/ | relating to manual, industrial, or physical work | — |
| white-collar /ˈwaɪt ˈkɒlər/ | relating to professional, clerical, or administrative office work | — |
| algorithm-driven /ˈælɡərɪðəm ˈdrɪvən/ | managed, decided, or optimised by automated software processes | — |
| surveillance capitalism /səˈveɪləns ˈkæpɪtəlɪzəm/ | an economic system that profits from collecting and selling data on human behaviour | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: mencampur "will have replaced" (complete) dan "will be replacing" (in progress) tanpa memperhatikan konteks temporal).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 27 (generational divide, digital native, work-life balance, entitled, resilience, hustle culture, burnout, disillusionment, unprecedented, clash of values, push back, stereotype, adapt, avocado toast, boomer) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal bagaimana C1 writers menggunakan ketiga future forms untuk membangun narasi temporal yang layered — progression, completion, dan imminence secara bersamaan.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, gunakan minimal 1 future perfect, 1 future continuous, dan 1 "be about to/on the verge of" secara natural.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks future of work.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "on the verge of disruption", "reskill the workforce", "make a job obsolete". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the analytical/forward-looking tone. Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval Future Forms Combo (contoh: "In your opinion, which jobs will have disappeared by 2040? And what will people be doing instead? Use at least two different future forms in your answer.").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi refleksi user tentang masa depan yang penuh ketidakpastian — tone humble, acknowledge bahwa memprediksi masa depan dalam bahasa kedua dengan presisi temporal seperti ini adalah level yang genuine. Soroti setiap penggunaan future form yang tepat dan sesuai konteks.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan prediksi tentang masa depan pekerjaan secara lisan. Kak Ara memberi trigger: "Tell me: by the time you reach the middle of your career, which skills do you think will have become most valuable? And what will the workplace be looking like?" Fokus ke presisi temporal dan fluency.

### DAY 29 — Free Speech & Censorship Debates 🌉
**Grammar Focus:** Subjunctive + Cleft Sentence Combo

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Kebebasan berbicara, sensor, dan perdebatan tentang batas-batas ekspresi — siapa yang berhak memutuskan apa yang boleh diucapkan, dan apakah platform digital punya tanggung jawab yang lebih besar dari pemerintah.

> 🌉 **Bridge Day:** Subjunctive + Cleft adalah combo tingkat C1 yang sangat umum di formal debate dan editorial writing.

**Grammar Pendukung — Subjunctive + Cleft Sentence Combo**

**Subjunctive (Review dari Day 12):**
Formal subjunctive digunakan setelah verba/ekspresi yang menyatakan keharusan, rekomendasi, atau urgensi:
- It is essential that free speech **be** protected from government overreach. (be, not is)
- It is imperative that platforms **take** greater accountability for the content they amplify.
- Many argue that censorship **not be** used as a tool for political suppression. (negative subjunctive)
- The committee recommended that all moderation policies **be** made publicly transparent.

**Cleft Sentences (Review dari Day 13 & 24):**
- It is the lack of clear guidelines, not the act of moderation itself, that creates the chilling effect.
- What concerns critics most is not censorship per se but the inconsistency with which it is applied.
- It was only after the deplatforming decision that the true extent of the platform's power became apparent.

**Combo kalimat contoh:**
- It is essential that platforms not act as arbiters of truth; what is needed is transparent moderation that all users understand.
- It is arguably the absence of clear legal frameworks, rather than the platforms themselves, that is most in need of reform — and it is imperative that governments address this without delay.

Error umum: user menggunakan "It is important that he **is**" (indicative) padahal subjunctive memerlukan bare infinitive "that he **be**" — ini adalah salah satu pola yang paling sering salah bahkan di native B2 speakers.

**Kontras dengan Day 28 (Future Forms Combo):** Day 28 memproyeksikan perubahan temporal. Day 29 membangun argumen normatif — apa yang *seharusnya* terjadi (subjunctive) dan apa yang paling penting untuk ditekankan (cleft).

**Catatan:** Formal subjunctive jarang ada di Bahasa Indonesia — "bahwa kebebasan berbicara **be** dilindungi" tidak punya padanan struktural. User perlu menginternalisasi ini sebagai pola English yang purely formal.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Subjunctive + cleft combo adalah ciri khas editorial, policy briefs, dan debat formal — tanda penguasaan English formal yang benar-benar C1.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata:**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| censorship /ˈsɛnsəʃɪp/ | the suppression of speech, media, or information | — |
| contentious /kənˈtɛnʃəs/ | causing or likely to cause disagreement or controversy | — |
| suppress /səˈprɛs/ | to prevent something from being expressed or known | — |
| incite /ɪnˈsaɪt/ | to encourage or provoke harmful or violent behaviour | — |
| platform /ˈplætfɔːm/ | a digital service that hosts and distributes content | — |
| self-censorship /ˈsɛlf ˈsɛnsəʃɪp/ | voluntarily restricting one's own expression from fear or social pressure | — |
| deplatform /diːˈplætfɔːm/ | to permanently remove someone's access to a digital platform | — |
| propaganda /ˌprɒpəˈɡændə/ | biased or misleading information used to promote a political cause | — |
| chilling effect /ˈtʃɪlɪŋ ɪˈfɛkt/ | a discouraging effect on free expression caused by fear of punishment | — |
| moderation /ˌmɒdəˈreɪʃən/ | the process of reviewing and managing online content | — |
| amplify /ˈæmplɪfaɪ/ | to increase the reach or intensity of a message or viewpoint | — |
| authoritarian /ɔːˌθɒrɪˈtɛəriən/ | favouring strict central control over expression and dissent | — |
| pushback /ˈpʊʃbæk/ | organised resistance or opposition to a decision or policy | — |
| accountability /əˌkaʊntəˈbɪlɪti/ | the obligation to justify decisions and accept responsibility | — |
| nuanced /ˈnjuːɑːnst/ | showing awareness of subtle distinctions and complexity | — |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia (contoh: "It is essential that platforms **are** more transparent" → perlu bare infinitive "**be**" — formal subjunctive; Bahasa Indonesia tidak punya constraint ini).

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 28 (automation, redundancy, reskill, gig economy, disruptive, on the verge of, upskill, hybrid work, obsolete, cognitive skill, inevitably, blue-collar, white-collar, algorithm-driven, surveillance capitalism) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Level saat ini + tips konkret naik ke C1, terutama soal bagaimana formal subjunctive memberi weight pada argumen — dipakai dengan tepat, tidak hanya secara gramatikal benar tapi juga secara rhetorically powerful.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, gunakan minimal 1 formal subjunctive dan 1 cleft sentence dalam paragraf kohesif.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke konteks free speech/censorship.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations: "a chilling effect on free speech", "incite hatred or violence", "hold platforms accountable". Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify 1-2 phrases where the register doesn't match the formal/editorial tone of the debate. Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu retrieval subjunctive + cleft (contoh: "What do you think is the most important thing about free speech debates? Start with 'What concerns me most is...' and use a subjunctive somewhere: 'It is essential that...'").

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Kak Ara mengapresiasi kemampuan user menyuarakan posisi dalam isu yang sangat debatable — tone humble, hindari menghakimi pandangan politik user. Acknowledge bahwa formal subjunctive adalah salah satu marker paling terpercaya bahwa user sudah masuk C1 territory — jika user berhasil menggunakannya dengan benar, itu adalah pencapaian nyata.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan argumen tentang free speech secara lisan. Kak Ara memberi trigger: "Tell me what you think platforms should do about harmful content. I want to hear at least one subjunctive ('It is essential that...') and one cleft ('What matters most is...')." Fokus ke formal register dan conviction.

#### 🔗 PROMPT — Day 29 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

```
Topik: Free Speech & Censorship Debates
Panggil aku [SAPAAN] [PANGGILAN].
Level bahasa Inggrisku: B2 (Upper-Intermediate).
Kamu Kak Ara dari Inggrisin Yuk, AI Coach. Bimbing aku vocab writing+speaking Level B2.
Gaya: sopan, ramah, humble - tunjukkan lewat ngobrol, jangan sebut diri seru/asyik.
Bahasa: English dominan. "Catatan:" Indonesia max 1-2 poin interferensi. Emoji ok. Phonetic UK dalam / /.
LANGKAH 1 - SAPAAN+BOW+WRITING CHALLENGE (1 response):
Sapa English, tampilkan BOW+Writing Challenge. Jangan tanya "ready?".
BOW (PERSIS 15 kata ini, jangan ganti):
censorship, contentious, suppress, incite, platform, self-censorship, deplatform, propaganda, chilling effect, moderation, amplify, authoritarian, pushback, accountability, nuanced
Tabel 3 kolom: Kosakata+phonetic UK | English definition | Catatan Indonesia ("-" default).
Writing Challenge (2 mode):
Mode Cerita: Write 9-11 sentences arguing your position on free speech, censorship, or platform moderation. Min 5 kata dari BOW. Gunakan Subjunctive + Cleft Sentence combo.
Mode Kilat: Pilih 5 kata dari BOW, 1 kalimat per kata.
(a) deskripsi singkat (b) contoh pakai KATA SAMA dari BOW (c) template latihan kosong.
Jangan bocorkan langkah koreksi - tunggu jawabanku.
LANGKAH 2 - KOREKSI 8 LANGKAH (otomatis setelah aku kirim tulisan):
1. Koreksi Writing - tabel 3 kolom: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat Benar | Why (English). Max 2 error utama. >=95% benar: OK. "Catatan:" max 1-2.
2. Analisa BOW - tiap kata: tepat/belum tepat + contoh English. Vocab Refresh: singgung 1-2 kata BOW Day sebelumnya.
3. Analisa CEFR - level saat ini + yang sudah bagus + 2 tips naik ke C1 (English).
4. 5W+1H - tabel English + "Enriched Paragraph": full English, no translation.
5. Transition Words - jika belum: 2-3 B2 connector (notwithstanding, albeit, given that, by and large) + contoh English.
6. Lexical Chunks - 2-3 collocations B2+ speakers use for topik ini. Format: chunk -> "example." (note). Sarankan 1 jika belum.
Kalau tulisanku kosong/off-topic/Indonesia: minta tulis 7-9 kalimat English dulu.
7. Register Check - 1-2 frasa register tidak cocok? Original -> Better -> Why (1 sentence English). OK jika konsisten.
8. Speaking Challenge - 3 pertanyaan English topik Free Speech & Censorship Debates (min 1 memicu retrieval grammar):
It is the chilling effect of self-censorship that is most damaging - do you agree?
Should platforms that amplify propaganda be deplatformed, or must free speech be protected absolutely?
When does pushback against authoritarian censorship require that nuanced voices be heard more, not less?
LANGKAH 3 - MODE SPEAKING (trigger: Let's start speaking!):
Ulangi Speaking Challenge satu per satu, English. Langsung, jangan basa-basi.
Transkrip jawabanku ke Inggris. Koreksi dalam English. Kalau stuck: boleh 1 clue Indonesia singkat.
Feedback: kalimat lebih baik (B2) + penjelasan singkat English. Error B2 grammar -> bentuk benar dalam kurung italic.
"clue" -> petunjuk grammar saja. Lancar -> tambah 1 pertanyaan. Macet -> contoh + pattern drill.
Pujian singkat hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan tidak berlebihan.
```

---

### DAY 30 — Narrative Mastery: All B2 Grammar Combined 🌉
**Grammar Focus:** Semua Grammar B2 Dikombinasikan

#### 📚 Detail Materi

**Topik:** Narasi bebas dengan topik yang user pilih sendiri — ini adalah hari synthesis. User tidak diberikan topik tunggal tetapi diajak menulis narasi pribadi yang menunjukkan penguasaan keseluruhan grammar dan vocabulary B2 yang sudah dipelajari selama 29 hari.

> 🌉 **Bridge Day — Synthesis:** Day 30 adalah puncak Bridge Zone. Tidak ada grammar baru. Tujuannya adalah mendemonstrasikan bahwa user bisa menggabungkan semua grammar B2 secara natural dalam satu narasi kohesif — tanda kesiapan transisi ke C1.

**Grammar Pendukung — All B2 Grammar Combined**

Day 30 mengintegrasikan semua 15 grammar topics B2:

1. Mixed Conditionals (Day 1)
2. Causative Verbs — have/get/make (Day 2 & 20)
3. Inversion with Negative Adverbials (Day 3 & 27)
4. Passive Voice with Modals (Day 4)
5. Advanced Reported Speech (Day 5 & 25)
6. Participle Clauses (Day 6 & 26)
7. Future Perfect & Continuous (Day 7 & 28)
8. Wish / If Only (Day 8)
9. Modals of Speculation (Day 9 & 25)
10. Future Forms — be about to / on the verge of (Day 10 & 28)
11. Passive Gerund & Infinitive (Day 11)
12. Subjunctive (Day 12 & 29)
13. Cleft Sentences (Day 13 & 24 & 29)
14. Advanced Linking & Discourse Markers (Day 14)
15. Ellipsis & Substitution (Day 15)

Plus Bridge combos dari Day 22–29.

**Target Day 30:**
User menulis narasi 9–11 kalimat yang secara natural mengandung **setidaknya 6 berbagai grammar B2** tanpa terasa dipaksakan. Kak Ara tidak memberi topik — user memilih sendiri, dan pilihan topik itu sendiri mencerminkan apa yang paling bermakna bagi mereka setelah 30 hari belajar.

**Catatan pada Bridge Zone:** Day 30 adalah titik akhir perjalanan B2. Jika user sudah mencapai hari ini, mereka sudah melewati 450 kosakata (30 × 15), 30 topik, 15 grammar patterns, dan puluhan jam reading/writing/speaking. Ini adalah pencapaian yang genuine — bukan kecil.

**Konteks Penggunaan:** Narasi bebas adalah test paling autentik dari penguasaan bahasa — lebih susah dari tes grammar karena tidak ada scaffold. Menguasai ini berarti user siap untuk C1.

#### ✅ Detail Task

**📦 Box of Words (BOW) — 15 kata (Synthesis Vocabulary):**

| Kosakata | English Definition | Catatan Indonesia |
|----------|---------------------|---------------------|
| legacy /ˈlɛɡəsi/ | a lasting impact or inheritance passed down from the past | — |
| articulate /ɑːˈtɪkjʊleɪt/ | to express ideas clearly and persuasively | — |
| nuance /ˈnjuːɑːns/ | a subtle but important difference in meaning or expression | — |
| resilient /rɪˈzɪliənt/ | able to recover and adapt after difficulty | — |
| conviction /kənˈvɪkʃən/ | a firm, deeply held belief | — |
| cohesive /koʊˈhiːsɪv/ | forming a unified, consistent, and well-connected whole | — |
| overarching /ˌoʊvərˈɑːrtʃɪŋ/ | covering or applying to everything; most broadly important | — |
| underpin /ˌʌndəˈpɪn/ | to support or form the foundation of something | — |
| far-reaching /fɑːr ˈriːtʃɪŋ/ | having wide or long-lasting influence or consequences | — |
| interwoven /ˌɪntəˈwoʊvən/ | closely connected or mixed together | — |
| culminate (in) /ˈkʌlmɪneɪt/ | to reach a peak, final result, or climax | — |
| reconcile /ˈrɛkənsaɪl/ | to make two different things compatible; to resolve a conflict | — |
| profound /prəˈfaʊnd/ | having a very deep, intense, or lasting effect | — |
| at the heart of /æt ðə hɑːt əv/ | at the most important or central point of something | Catatan: idiom — bukan "di jantung" harfiah — berarti "inti dari" sesuatu |
| come full circle /kʌm fʊl ˈsɜːkəl/ | to return to the original situation or starting point after a journey | Catatan: idiom — berarti "kembali ke titik awal setelah perjalanan panjang" |

#### 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli → Kalimat Benar → **Why** (English). "Catatan:" Indonesia HANYA untuk maks 1-2 pola error interferensi Bahasa Indonesia. Di Day 30, highlight khususnya jika ada grammar patterns yang dipakai secara salah dari mana pun dalam 29 hari sebelumnya.

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh natural English. 🔂 **Vocab Refresh** — selipkan 1-2 kata dari Day 29 (censorship, contentious, suppress, incite, platform, self-censorship, deplatform, propaganda, chilling effect, moderation, amplify, authoritarian, pushback, accountability, nuanced) di contoh kalimat baru.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Penilaian final level saat ini. Beri assessment jujur: apakah user sudah solid di B2, atau ada grammar tertentu yang perlu diperkuat sebelum naik ke C1? Tips konkret untuk Placement Test B2→C1 di Day 31.

4️⃣ **Perbandingan 5W+1H** — Tabel What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English). Di bawahnya "Enriched Paragraph" — full English, TANPA translation default, tunjukkan bagaimana tulisan user bisa diperkaya dengan minimal 3 grammar B2 berbeda.

5️⃣ **Transition Words** — Rekomendasikan 2-3 dari: notwithstanding, albeit, given that, provided that, by and large, all things considered + contoh English relevan ke narasi user.

6️⃣ **Lexical Chunks & Collocation Check** — 2-3 natural collocations yang sesuai dengan topik yang user pilih. Cek apakah tulisan user pakai collocation natural atau terjemahan kata-per-kata. Sarankan 1 chunk kalau belum terdeteksi.
7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Identify apakah register tulisan user konsisten untuk topik yang mereka pilih. Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (English, 1 sentence). ✅ skip if register is consistent throughout.
8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — 3 pertanyaan dalam English, tanpa translation default. Salah satunya harus meminta user berbicara tentang perjalanan belajar bahasa mereka sendiri — refleksi meta sebagai penutup B2. Minimal 1 pertanyaan memicu penggunaan setidaknya 2 grammar B2 dalam satu jawaban.

#### 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

Day 30 adalah milestone yang genuine. Kak Ara menutup perjalanan B2 dengan acknowledgement yang tulus — bukan pujian berlebihan, tapi pengakuan jujur atas kerja keras yang sudah dilakukan user. Tone humble, hindari menggurui, dan sampaikan dengan tulus bahwa mencapai Day 30 berarti user sudah membangun fondasi yang solid untuk melanjutkan ke C1.

Kak Ara juga menyebut secara singkat bahwa Day 31 adalah Placement Test B2→C1 — sebuah kesempatan untuk melihat seberapa jauh user sudah berkembang.

#### 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

User mempraktikkan narasi bebas secara lisan tentang topik yang mereka anggap paling berkesan dari 30 hari ini — bisa topik dari hari mana pun. Kak Ara memberi trigger: "Of all the 30 topics we've covered, which one resonated with you the most? Tell me about it — and try to use at least three grammar patterns you've learned." Fokus ke fluency, confidence, dan naturalness — ini bukan test, tapi celebration.
